 • If the video keeps pausing or is low quality, try restarting the video and rebooting your device. You can resume where you left off.
 
 • On some phones, it might take a minute after the video starts for the quality of both the video and the audio to stabilize. • On some phones, it might take a minute after the video starts for the quality of both the video and the audio to stabilize. This can happen each time you jump to a different time in the video.
 
 • If you’re streaming on a mobile cellular network, you might be connected to a slower network. For example, Edge is slower than 3G, and 3G is slower than 4G or LTE.
 
 • If you’re using a public Wi-Fi connection, other computers and devices connected to the same Internet connection can reduce the available bandwidth for video streaming.
 
 • If you’re using a home Wi-Fi connection, stop file transfers and audio/video streaming on other devices on your home network. You can also try restarting your Internet modem or router to ensure you have the best possible connection to your Internet service provider (ISP).
 
 • If there’s no sound with your video, check your device’s volume setting to ensure it’s not turned all the way down. If you’re using headphones, ensure your headphones are snugly connected. If you have a Bluetooth headset turned on, check to see if your audio is being sent there, or try disabling Bluetooth."</string>

    <string name="one_click_settings_about_text">When Mobile 1–Click is enabled, you will be able to purchase physical items from your mobile device with the click of only one button. You won’t be required to sign in every time you make a purchase. 1–Click ordering is always used to purchase digital items, such as digital videos, digital music and apps If you click to buy a digital item, it will automatically be charged to the default payment method on your account. Turning off Mobile 1–Click does not turn off 1–Click ordering for digital items. &lt;br/> &lt;br/> Mobile 1–Click on your mobile device is a separate feature from the 1–Click feature you use on your computer. Each setting may be turned on or off independent of the other. However, your default address and payment methods are the same for Mobile 1–Click, the 1–Click feature you use with your computer, and 1–Click ordering for digital items. &lt;br/> &lt;br/> Mobile 1–Click may only be turned on from your mobile device. Your Mobile 1–Click settings are only viewable from your computer if you have Mobile 1–Click activated. &lt;br/> &lt;br/> You can turn off Mobile 1–Click from the Your Account feature on either your mobile device or your computer.</string>
